<tr><td><h3><a href="https://github.com/aopp286/djy/blob/master/gb/20/4/15/n12032643.md#1" target="_blank">西藏林芝森林山火蔓延3个山头 浓烟四起</a><br></h3><a href="https://github.com/aopp286/djy/blob/master/gb/20/4/15/n12032643.md#1" target="_blank"><img width="150" src="https://i.epochtimes.com/assets/uploads/2020/04/2020-04-15_17-09-32-150x120.jpg" align ="left"></a>4月14日17时35分，西藏林芝市巴宜区尼西村发生森林火灾，过火地包括三座山头。火场海拔3100余米，山高坡陡。
